Easterner’s Mischievous Prank: Manure Placed on Beauty's Head, Yu Youxin Slapped Twice, Shen Hongbao Quickly Chased and Caught the Thug 166

Shen Jianqing, a Shaoxing native residing at No. 11 Xue Alley in this city, is 55 years old. Shen has two daughters, the elder, Hongbao, is 17, and the younger, Lübao, is 14. There was a fellow named Yu Youxin, 27 years old, from Huizhou, working at the bone tile workshop at No. 5 Zhangjia Alley. Because of his short stature, people often called him "Easterner." He lived not far from the Shen family, and Yu became acquainted with Hongbao and others, often visiting them. One evening around 5 p.m. on the 7th of this month, Hongbao and Lübao, the two sisters, having just finished bathing due to the intense heat, were sitting in front of the door, trying to cool off. At that moment, Yu Youxin (nicknamed "Easterner") happened to be at the doorway, flipping through a small picture book, "(Wang Wuneng Captures Ding Guaiguai)," which Lübao saw and wanted to borrow to take a look. However, Yu refused, triggering Lübao's anger, and a quarrel ensued. Seeing this, Hongbao suddenly stepped forward and slapped Yu twice. Afterward, Yu, not to be outdone, threw a punch, and the two sides erupted into a scuffle. Neighbors came out to mediate, and the dispute subsided. But Yu was still not satisfied. He gathered more than twenty rogue acquaintances and rushed to the Shen's house, intending to drag Shen's father, Jianqing, to a teahouse for a discussion and judgment. However, Shen happened to be out and had not returned, so they couldn't find him, and they dispersed in frustration. Then, yesterday morning around 9 a.m., Hongbao was embroidering shoe uppers at the doorway when, unexpectedly, the Easterner suddenly arrived, holding a cigarette paper box filled with manure, and dumped it on her head. Hongbao was caught off guard, and her head, face, and clothes were stained with manure, emitting a foul odor. Yu took the opportunity to escape, but Hongbao took off the manure-filled box and chased after him, grabbing and restraining him. She called for Zhang Xuemin, the watchman of the 29th post, who brought him to the Second Precinct of the First District. After preliminary interrogation by Chief Liu, the case was deemed a mischievous prank, and a document was prepared and submitted to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for further investigation.

Son Dies for Father: Father Fails to Repay Debt, Son Driven to Suicide 167

Xu Pengyun, 24 years old, from Yuyao, Zhejiang, is currently an apprentice at the Shanghai Wei Ye Silver Company at No. 631 Wangjia Sha, Baike Road. His father, Xu Zhihang, 46 years old, frequently travels between Shanghai and Ningbo, trading goods. Recently, he collected straw hat brims in Shanghai and transported them to Ningbo to be woven into straw hats, which he then sold in Shanghai. Xu Pengyun guaranteed all the Shanghai payments. Now, because his father has been irresponsible and has not repaid the debts, the creditors are pressing Xu Pengyun, the guarantor, for repayment. Pengyun, burdened by his father's bad behavior and unable to repay, felt driven to despair. The night before last, he bought poison and checked into Room 5 of the Yuanfa Inn at No. 13 Dongxin Bridge Street in the French Concession at 4:15 a.m. yesterday. He instructed the tea server to wake him up at 1:30 p.m., then closed the door and lay down to sleep, taking the poison and committing suicide. At 1:30 p.m. yesterday, the tea server, Yao Genfa, knocked on the door as instructed, but there was no response. Suspecting something was wrong, he pried open the door and went inside, only to find Xu dead on the bed. When Xu checked into the inn, he used the alias Xu Xianding, 22 years old, from Suzhou, a dealer in foreign goods. The inn reported the incident to the police station, which dispatched detectives to investigate. Beside the deceased, several business cards were found. The body was sent to the Tongren Fuyuan Branch for autopsy. Subsequently, according to the address on the business cards, his younger brother, Xu Guangyou, was found working as an apprentice at the Feilong Leather Goods Company at No. 4 Meibaike Road. After questioning Xu, his true name and the reason for his suicide were revealed. His father in Ningbo is still unaware that his son committed suicide due to being implicated in his debts. It is now scheduled that the Special No. 2 District Court will be notified today to send personnel for inspection, after which the family will collect the body for burial.

Chinese Buddhist Association Requests Approval to Send Members to Various Prisons to Propagate Buddhism and Transform Inmates into Good Citizens 168

Yesterday, the Chinese Buddhist Association sent a letter to Ju Zheng, President of the Judicial Yuan, saying: "President Ju Juegong, Judicial Yuan, greetings. With the arrival of spring and the renewal of governance, we respectfully admire your clear judgment and compassionate heart. Upholding the law with impartiality, just as the Lü Criminal Code, and removing the harshness of the Qin dynasty laws, with compassion and not rejoicing, we offer our reverence and wish to serve. We respectfully report that before the year of Dingmao [1927], all provincial prisons had instructors, most of whom were Buddhists. At that time, most administrators also revered Buddhism, and the results were evident. Later, due to turbulent times, this practice was discontinued. People tend to be indifferent to Buddhist teachings in times of prosperity, but they begin to realize their value after experiencing setbacks. Applying Buddhist teachings to transform those who are incarcerated, allowing them to repent, is more effective. Even after they are released from prison, they can become good citizens of society. Recognizing this, our association has already petitioned your esteemed Yuan to issue a general order to the courts of all provinces, cities, and counties, allowing Buddhist organizations to select teachers to propagate Buddhism in various prisons for the purpose of transformation. We are sending a copy of the draft to you for your review. If you grant approval, the benefits to the prisoners will be immeasurable."

New Development of the Datong Music Society: Using Yuan Dynasty System to Worship Confucius 172

Since the large-scale Confucius worship ceremony held in Tokyo, Japan, this spring, its unprecedented grandeur has greatly shocked people's hearts. Confucius is China's Confucius, not Japan's. If they respect him so much, then we should strive to be ahead and not lag behind. This is a definite principle. Now, our national government has issued an order the other day, setting August 27 as Confucius's birthday. With the government advocating at the top, all our people should respond at the bottom and actively participate, surpassing Japan if possible, so as not to be ashamed of the true spirit of our Chinese nation. According to research, the Confucius worship ceremony of the Yuan Dynasty was the most grand in our country's history. The number of dancers was large, and the musical instruments used included both elegant and popular styles. The dance had nine sections. The Ming and Qing dynasties only used six sections. The music score is called Dasheng Music (i.e., Zhonghe Shaoyue). The Datong Music Society in this city has been collecting it for a long time and used it once at the memorial service for the martyrs of the Shanghai War last year. It was solemn and different from the others. Now, the society plans to take advantage of this opportunity to convene all its new and old members, unite with the various national music groups in Shanghai to cooperate, and follow the Yuan Dynasty's method. In addition to the elegant musical instruments, they will also display various special musical instruments from around the world, inserting harmonies and uniformly using them to create a large-scale performance, opening up a new era for elegant music. Regarding the dance problem, they are planning to discuss it with one or two middle schools to undertake the task, with a deadline of one month for training. As for the displayed sacrificial offerings, such as grains, vegetables, fruits, livestock, game, aquatic products, etc., which are all the needs of human life passed down by the sages and on which the success or failure of politics depends, they are also planning to exhibit them all, so that the true picture of our country's five thousand years of etiquette and music can be seen. This move concerns the foundation of the nation and is by no means superficial. All of us in various circles should actively participate and contribute to this grand event, so that we will not lag behind Japan again. It is said that the society has already begun preparations.

Gift Certificates Issued by Banks Must Be Affixed with Stamps According to Ministry Order; Bankers Association Notifies All Banks, to Be Implemented Starting Today 173

The gift certificates issued by various banks in this city have never been affixed with stamps. Now, the Ministry of Finance has ordered that all must be affixed with stamps in accordance with the Stamp Tax Regulations, or they will be banned. The banks believe that this measure is unprecedented, so many are taking a wait-and-see attitude. Now, after the Bankers Association convened the 48th Executive Committee meeting for discussion, it officially notified all banks yesterday, instructing them to comply with the Ministry's order and affix stamps in accordance with the law. It is said that all banks have decided to start affixing stamps on gift certificates starting today. The original letter from the Bankers Association and the Stamp Tax Regulations are listed below:

Bankers Association Letter 174

Yesterday, the Bankers Association sent a letter to various banks in this city, saying: "We are writing to inform you that according to letters from Xinhua, Chouye, and Shanghai banks, they recently received a letter from the Ministry of Finance stating that the issuance of gift certificates should be affixed with stamps in accordance with Article 2, Category 2, Item 5 of the Stamp Tax Regulations, according to the progressive tax rate. The trade has not previously affixed stamps to gift certificates. Please reply as to whether we should comply with the order. After deliberation at the 48th Executive Committee meeting of this association, it was decided that although there is no clear provision in the Stamp Tax Regulations stating that gift certificates should be affixed with stamps, after studying their nature, they are quite similar to deposit receipts, and it is not inappropriate to apply the rules by analogy. In the future, stamps should be affixed in accordance with the deposit receipt article of the Stamp Tax Regulations, without omission. We hereby notify all banks in the same industry to be informed."

Stamps to Be Affixed 175

Bank gift certificates should be affixed with stamps according to the following progressive tax rates: For amounts of one yuan or more but less than ten yuan, affix a one-cent stamp; for ten yuan or more but less than one hundred yuan, affix a two-cent stamp; for one hundred yuan or more but less than five hundred yuan, affix a four-cent stamp; for five hundred yuan or more but less than one thousand yuan, affix a ten-cent stamp; for one thousand yuan or more but less than five thousand yuan, affix a twenty-cent stamp; for five thousand yuan or more but less than ten thousand yuan, affix a fifty-cent stamp; for ten thousand yuan or more but less than fifty thousand yuan, affix a one-yuan stamp; for fifty thousand yuan or more, affix a one-yuan and fifty-cent stamp; no additional stamps are required for amounts over fifty thousand yuan.

Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce Introduces Domestic Dyes Produced by Dachung 176

The dye industry has always been dominated by imported products. Most of the dyeing and weaving factories in our country use foreign goods because there are no domestic products. The annual outflow of capital is staggering, which is a major loss for our country. Mr. Dong Yuchang, an industrialist in Shanghai, founded the Dachung Dye Factory, and its vulcanized Yuanqing product can indeed compete with imported products. Yesterday, the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce introduced it to the chambers of commerce in various places for adoption, in order to promote domestic products. The original telegram is copied below: "To all municipal chambers of commerce across the country: We recently received a letter from Shanghai Dachung Dye Factory Co., Ltd., which reads, 'Our factory's Zhongzi trademark vulcanized Yuanqing dye is of excellent quality and low price, enough to compete with imported products and stop the outflow of capital. We have applied to the Ministry of Industry for examination and approval for exemption from production tax and forwarded it to the Ministry of Finance for execution. Since its production, it has been sold to various places and has been praised and purchased by dyeing and weaving factories and dye shops. Sales have been increasing day by day. We have always admired your association's efforts in promoting domestic products, and we hereby request you to forward it to chambers of commerce across the country for introduction,' etc. We have checked and found that dyes have always been dominated by imported products in the market. Now, the factory's vulcanized Yuanqing product can indeed compete with imported products. We are enclosing samples and sending a telegram to your association, hoping that you will check and forward it to dyeing and weaving factories and dye shops for introduction and adoption, in order to promote domestic products and stop the outflow of capital. We eagerly await your response. Lin Kanghou, Chairman of the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce, bows.'"

A Collection of Epidemic News 177

The Jiyi Epidemic Hospital on Tangshan Road, Hongkou, began providing consultations on the first of this month. Yesterday (the 8th) at 4 p.m., the official opening ceremony was held. More than 100 representatives from over 80 organizations, including the Municipal Government, the Health Bureau, the Social Affairs Bureau, the Ningbo Fellow Association, and the Chongyi Charity Association, attended. The president of the hospital, Bao Yaoting, presided over the meeting and reported in detail on the progress since the opening. The meeting adjourned at 6 p.m. Since the opening of the hospital, it has treated more than 4,000 patients, with heatstroke and dysentery being the most common. The Xizang Road Epidemic Hospital is currently treating about 200 patients a day. For example, there were 184 cases the day before yesterday and 193 cases as of 8 p.m. last night, with acute gastroenteritis (i.e., cholera) being the most common. However, no cases of true cholera have been found. It is reported that four people died yesterday due to lack of treatment.

The Emergency Epidemic Hospital at the intersection of Xizang Road and Kaifeng Road treated 114 cases yesterday, with 16 patients being hospitalized due to severe illness. The diseases were mostly heatstroke, dysentery, and gastroenteritis.

The Red Cross Epidemic Hospital on Xinmin Road, Zhabei, officially opened on the 7th. As of yesterday, it had treated more than 800 cases. Yesterday alone, it treated more than 300 cases, with more than 30 patients being hospitalized. More than 50 people came to the hospital for vaccination.

The World Bank held its third annual shareholders meeting in its new building yesterday. Opening of the Taifeng Company Tea and Snack Department 179

The Taifeng Canned Food Company on Nanjing Road, which pioneered the mechanized production of various foods, biscuits, candies, etc., is a well-known enterprise in our country. Yesterday (the 9th), the company's newly opened tea and snack department held its opening ceremony. In the morning, Mayor Wu, representing Yu Hongjun, unveiled the plaque. From 1 p.m. to 8 p.m. in the afternoon, reporters from various newspapers and guests from all walks of life were invited to visit and offer congratulations, with no less than six or seven hundred people attending. The company's general manager, Deng Ruiren, and Luo Jizhai and Su Yuming cordially received them and offered various homemade Chinese and Western snacks and cold drinks. There was a constant stream of vehicles and horses, making it a grand occasion. The decoration of the tea and snack department is quite elegant, and the seats are spacious. As for the food, it is particularly clean and hygienic, and the prices are low. Furthermore, old habits are abolished, and no tips are taken. The daily business hours are from 7 a.m. to 10 p.m., including Sundays. At the same time, the company's goods are sold at a large discount for ten days to celebrate the opening.

Assassination Case Behind Zhaofeng Garden: Female Culprit Identified from Young Girl's Testimony; Zhang Hanzhang Knocked Down Binnei; Lu Wangshi Has Confessed the Whole Story 180

On May 21st of this year, at about 9 p.m., a tragic assassination case occurred behind Zhaofeng Garden in Caojiadu. After receiving the report, the detective team of the Municipal Public Security Bureau immediately dispatched Deputy Squad Leader Dong Wenrui, leading detectives Wang Yixin, Yang Qing, and Wu Yihe, to rush to the

Page 14

scene. They surrounded the area to capture the murderer, but he had already escaped. It was found that the deceased was Qiang Fugeng, over 30 years old, from Wuxi, who ran a lace shop called Zhenchangxiang on Sanma Road. The main culprit was Zhang Hanzhang, who ran a butcher shop in Wujiaochang, Caojiadu. The female culprit was Lu Wangshi, the wife of Lu Yizhang, a Cantonese man who ran a Holland water company at No. 1 Tongqing Lane, Minguo Road. Since the incident, the team has been sending personnel to investigate the suspects every day, but without any trace. Detective Squad Leader Wu Kezhong found out that Lu Wangshi's brother, Wang Shushan, often went to Lu's house at No. 1 Tongqing Lane, Xiaobeimen, to secretly communicate information. Therefore, he sent Wang Yixin to guard the place secretly. There was indeed a clue. He reported the previous situation to Captain Lu and District Chief Tan of the Sixth District, and additional detectives were sent. At about 1 p.m. the day before yesterday, they, together with the First Section of the Second District, went to No. 1 Tongqing Lane to arrest Wang Shushan, but he was not found. Only Lu Wangshi's daughter, Lu Yirong, was taken into custody. She claimed to be 12 years old. At first, she did not admit anything, but after repeated questioning, she confessed that since the incident, her mother had been hiding at No. 10 Jianye Lane, Fuli Road, in the French Concession. Her father, Lu Yizhang, and her maternal uncle, Wang Shushan, were also living in the lane, etc. After obtaining the confession, they immediately joined the Songshan Road Police Station and went to the three-story building and arrested the female culprit, Lu Wangshi, and the suspects Lu Yizhang and Wang Shushan. After being brought to the district and interrogated, Lu Wangshi confessed that she was 31 years old and from Huzhou, Zhejiang. She directly admitted that at about 7 p.m. that afternoon, she and Qiang Fugeng went to the Youth Association Lane behind Zhaofeng Garden to ask Zhou Wenbo for 50 yuan to repay Zhang Hanzhang's interest because she guaranteed Qiang Fugeng's debt of 500 yuan to Zhang Hanzhang. Unexpectedly, Zhou Wenbo had moved earlier. So, they returned. When walking on the small stone bridge of the Youth Association Lane, they saw three or five people coming towards them. Suddenly, Zhang Hanzhang knocked Qiang Fugeng down into the Binnei River. Zhang Hanzhang told me to take a rickshaw and leave first. Then, Zhang Hanzhang caught up and also took a rickshaw to Wujiaochang, where they hired a car and rode together to Dongxin Bridge, where they got off and dispersed separately. I don't know the details of what happened afterward. The district deemed the case to be an assassination and ordered that the four suspects, including Lu Wangshi, be sent to the headquarters for legal action yesterday.

The Women's Apartment, affiliated with the Shanghai Chinese Women's Temperance Association and located at the intersection of Luban Road and Bubu Road in the French Concession, is organizing a summer lecture series to enhance knowledge and cultivate character. Chinese Zheng Ruyi Invents Scientific Building Materials, Striving to Counter Foreign Goods and Prevent Outflow of Capital 182

Nine out of ten of our country's building materials rely on foreign countries, and domestic products are scarce. Chemist Zheng Ruyi, recognizing this, founded the Yali Manufacturing Factory three years ago to specialize in the manufacture of various domestic building materials, hoping to recover our rights and interests. The number of products has now increased to twelve. The first two products to be launched, Waterproofing Paste and Transparent Waterproofing Paint, have caused similar imported goods to disappear from the market and have greatly impacted oil felt. The factory has three new products, which are introduced as follows:

Colloidal Oil: Most cement roofs use oil felt, which is not only expensive and labor-intensive but also black and uneven, and the material is heavy. Colloidal oil is a thin chemical oil. When used, it only needs to be applied to a cement surface, and it can penetrate into the micropores and seal them. As for the shape of the roof, it does not change. The price is extremely low, only four or five yuan per square meter.

Waterproofing Paint: It is very difficult to repair leaking cement roofs because cement mortar is ineffective. With the advent of Waterproofing Paste, this problem can be easily solved. It can repair any leaking cement, white iron, or oil felt roof, platform, etc., with a single brush, which is very convenient.

Wood Preservative Oil: Wood Preservative Oil can make wood resistant to insects and durable. It can be used alone or mixed with tung oil. It is a preservative for wood piles, boats, and building timber. Its selling price is one-third lower than similar imported products on the market. It is also reported that in order to promote business, the factory has sent business director Jin to Hong Kong, Little Luzon, and the South Seas Islands to negotiate distribution.

Rickshaw Puller Assault Case Awaiting Judgment; Rickshaw Puller Demands Compensation of Eighty Yuan 183

Rickshaw puller Wang Yuzhen from Tongzhou and his companion Zhao Yutai from Jiangbei had a dispute over passengers at Wuchang Road at about 10 a.m. on the 13th of last month. They fought each other, and as a result, Zhao suffered a severe head injury and fell to the ground crying for help. The patrol police arrested Wang and took him to the Hongkou Police Station for detention. The injured person was sent to the hospital for treatment. His injuries were quite severe. The next morning, the police sent the suspect Wang to the First Special District Court for adjudication pending the recovery of the victim. The other day, Judge Wu Zehan visited the Third Criminal Court for a further hearing. Lawyer Li Zhi of the Public Works Department said that the plaintiff's injury has slightly recovered and there is no danger to his life. He came to court to testify. According to Zhao Yutai's statement, his family is poor. Since being injured by the defendant, he has been unable to pull a rickshaw, and life has been difficult. He demanded compensation of eighty yuan for his losses and did not pursue the criminal part. When questioned, the defendant admitted that he had no money to pay and could at most raise twenty yuan for negotiation. The judge, Zhao, insisted on the above amount. Judge Wu ordered that he be remanded in custody, and the sentence will be announced on schedule.

Seaman Tang Xiangjun's Body Found Floating 184

Tang Xiangjun, 27 years old, from Ningbo, was a sailor on the Jianghai Customs Haiguang ferry. At 2:45 p.m. on the 6th of this month, Tang was working on the side of the Haiguang ferry in Zhao Xingde's sampan No. 71, clearing the water pipes when a ship entered the port and passed by the Haiguang ferry. Suddenly, waves splashed, shaking the sampan, and Tang Xiangjun was knocked into the river. He drowned immediately and did not resurface. Although efforts were made to salvage him, there was no trace of his body. Until 5 p.m. the day before yesterday, Tang Xiangjun's body floated up in the river at the Hongsheng Wharf in Pudong. The rescue bureau patrol boat took him to the South Wharf to await inspection. Yesterday morning, the Water Patrol Police Station prepared a letter and sent Detective Xu Lenian, along with witnesses Shen Dingdong, the fourth steward of the Haiguang ferry, and Zhao Xingde, the owner of the sampan, to the Local Court to request an autopsy. Prosecutor Tang Ruxiu examined the case and ordered that they go to the mortuary to wait. Soon after, Prosecutor Tang, along with the coroner, went to the South Wharf and confirmed that the deceased Tang Xiangjun had indeed drowned in the river. He filled out the death certificate and ordered the family to collect the coffin and wait for instructions. It is learned that the deceased Tang Xiangjun, also known as Agen, lost his father at a young age. He was originally from Ningbo. His family includes an elderly mother in her sixties, a wife, and a four-year-old daughter, as well as a son born last June. The family of several people all relied on the deceased for a living.

Huang Laigui's Appeal Dismissed 185

Huang Laigui, 21 years old from Anhui, was previously a clerk at Yanqing Tang, a pickled melon shop on Xian Guagua Street in the South City. Previously, he stole and sold goods and then absconded with the money. After searching for him without success, the shop owner, Xu Hanming, published a notice urging him to come forward and settle the matter out of their fellow-villager relationship. However, after seeing the notice, Huang hired lawyer Fang Junjie and sued Xu Hanming in the Local Court for defamation and hired lawyers Zhu Xiyun and Zhu Zhizhong to defend him. After the court hearing, Xu Hanmin was acquitted. Huang, however, did not accept the verdict and appealed again. After two court hearings, the appeal was dismissed. This was because the court had already verified that the facts stated in the notice regarding Huang Laigui were accurate. Furthermore, the prosecutor had concluded the investigation of his illegal acts and had filed a public prosecution on May 16th of this year. During the appeal court hearing, Huang's testimony was completely inconsistent with that of his witness, Bao Caizhang, which was obviously fabricated. Therefore, the court held that the appellant's empty accusations could not be said to have reason and ruled to reject the appeal.

Further Investigation into the Tangshan Road Robbery Case 186

On the morning of the 2nd of this month, at 6:30 AM, the home of Wang Tangde, a Ningbo native residing at No. 134, Yuanji Lane, Tangshan Road, was broken into and robbed of valuables worth over one hundred yuan. In the past few days, Chinese and foreign detectives from the Huishan Police Station arrested the robbers, Ying Xingdao and Shen Agen, both Ningbo natives, along with women Shen Pan and Zhang Wang, at Zhaofeng Road and Rongfa Inn, Baoyu Lane, Dongxin Bridge in the French Concession. The following morning, they were sent to the First Special District Court. Li Zhishan, a lawyer from the Public Works Department, made a statement requesting an extension of their detention for further investigation. Wang Tangde, the victim, testified that he was out at the time and only found out upon returning home. According to his daughter, Meirong, three robbers entered through the back door, threatened them into silence, and stole six gold rings. When questioned, the defendants' statements were evasive. Judge Wu Zehan ordered them to be remanded in custody separately, with a revised date for further investigation.

The Efficacy of Two Famous Medicines from Jiufu Company. Buliduo Sheng Dan is one of the two major famous medicines of Jiufu Company and two major stars among new drugs. Buliduo effectively treats lung conditions and coughs and has long enjoyed a great reputation. Initially, there were only two pure types, but later, to fully treat all conditions, three more types were added: iodine, arsenic, and quinine, totaling five types with the original two, like the five fingers of a hand, each with its own function and specialty. Pure Buliduo is an excellent medicine for physical weakness and poor metabolism. Buliduo with quinine is an excellent medicine for colds, coughs, and tuberculosis. Buliduo with iodine is an excellent medicine for asthma, shortness of breath, syphilis, and scrofula. Buliduo with arsenic is an excellent medicine for blood deficiency, weak nerves, and chronic skin diseases. Buliduo with quinine is an excellent medicine for malnutrition, anemia, weak stomach, and post-illness weakness. Sheng Dan is essential for preventing and controlling epidemics and is the most effective preparation to replace imported pills. Recently, due to drought and lack of rain, epidemics are rampant. If everyone carries Sheng Dan with them, they can always ensure safety whether they are at home or away.

Letters to the Editor 194

To the esteemed Editor:

Regarding the news of Ms. Xia Xiaoqing receiving a Swiss flying license in our Geneva dispatch on the 3rd of this month, after investigation, Ms. Li is the wife of Mr. Zheng Baifeng, Secretary of the League of Nations. Due to an omission in the telegram, the two characters (Baifeng) were mistranslated. We hereby urgently correct this error and request that you publish this correction in your newspaper. Sincerely, Shanghai Branch of the Central News Agency, July 9.

Sir,

We, Ni Qiusheng, et al., claim that because the Xin Pudong Bao and the Pudong Xing Bao published news about (Tongxing Clothing Store operating a gambling den) and (Zhoupu Gambling Case), we, being law-abiding merchants, have never engaged in such illegal activities. Therefore, we filed a private prosecution and the First Special District Court held a hearing on July 7th, before advising a postponement for a further hearing. However, upon reading the news item (Two Pudong Newspapers Sued) published in the Shen Bao on July 9th, which contains entirely one-sided statements, we fear that misinformation will lead to further misinformation and confuse the public. We therefore request that you write a letter to the Shen Bao to clarify that these statements should be published in the "Letters to the Editor" column to correct the record, etc. Therefore, we are writing on their behalf, requesting that you investigate and handle this matter. Respectfully, to the Editor of the Shen Bao, Lawyer Wang Tiehua.

Sir,

Having read a news item titled "Villagers Seeking Rain Cause Trouble" in your newspaper on July 7th, after checking with the report of Gu Xianchun, the independent platoon leader of our district regiment, we have found some discrepancies. We are writing to correct these discrepancies. It was found that members of the platoon, in an effort to maintain order, were stabbed by thugs. Platoon member Pan Yiqin (mistakenly published as Pan Huicheng) was robbed of a 6-inch handgun (No. 964) while in pain. The gun's magazine has been retrieved by villager Xu Abu and handed over to the Public Security Bureau of the Sixth District for investigation. In addition, platoon members Gu Zhaopeng (mistakenly identified as Gu Zhaotang), Xu Zhongying, and Zou Liukang all suffered injuries to their backs and faces. Two suspects have already been apprehended, and we have petitioned the superiors to investigate the matter. We hereby correct the record and request that this correction be published in the "Letters to the Editor" column to ensure accuracy. Respectfully, Shanghai Pusong District Defense Regiment, July 7.

Reading News | Edited by the Reading Guidance Department of the Shen Bao Circulation Library 195

Table of Contents:

(1) Introduction to 20 Good Summer Reads

(2) Important Mailbox - 3 Items

(1) 20 Good Summer Reads. Many readers have written requesting special reading guidance for the summer. This is because it is too hot in the summer, and it is difficult to read difficult books. Some readers are students with summer vacations, and even friends working in offices may not work in the afternoons. There is a lot of free time, so you can leisurely read some books. Other friends who are busy 12 hours a day cannot talk about summer rest, but the climate will definitely affect their lives. In the summer, everyone wants to find something refreshing to adjust their lives. Therefore, the last issue of this journal asked readers for their opinions on summer reading materials. This week, we have received many enthusiastic submissions from readers, and we have received a lot of materials. Now, referring to everyone's opinions, we have selected 20 books, divided into 10 literary works and 10 books of a social science nature, for summer study.

I. Literary Books:

1. *The Literary Mind and the Carving of Dragons* (Kaiming Edition)

2. *The Development History of European Literature and Art* (Kaiming Edition)

3. *The First Flag of Europe* (Chunguang Edition)

4. *In the Darkness* (Kaiming Edition)

5. *Seaward Bound* (Xingken Edition)

6. *All Quiet on the Western Front* (Guanghua Edition)

7. *Confessions* (World Edition)

8. *And That's All* (Beixin Edition)

(2) Mailbox

I. Please Enclose Postage for Mail Order (Reader Communication Cards). Recently, readers from both local and other cities have been sending mail orders for Reader Communication Cards to this department, but they have not enclosed postage, which has invisibly increased a small loss for this department. Because the pricing of the communication cards is entirely based on cost, and more than 200 books have been sold in other cities, the loss has reached more than 10 yuan, which has greatly affected the budget of this department. Now, we request that all readers, when ordering by mail from other cities in the future, please enclose 5 fen for postage, and for local cities, please enclose 2 fen. Those who have already received the communication cards from this department but have not yet enclosed postage are also requested to send it. Stamps are fully accepted. II. Solicitation of Criticism of Reading Materials. This library has thousands of books. There are often hundreds of books of the same nature. Among them, there are naturally many famous books worth reading carefully, but there are also inevitably some unhealthy foods that are still circulating outside, which makes us very uneasy. This department originally had a plan to accurately inspect the library's collection and practically take on the task of (book lending guidance). However, for several months, due to the shortage of manpower, although we have worked very hard, we have not been able to achieve even one-ten-thousandth of what we hoped for. Now we have decided to open this work to all readers and ask everyone to participate. For any books published in China, whether this library has them or not, after you have read them, whether the content is good or bad, or if you find any printing errors, please write them out clearly and send them to us for our reference. We also request that people across the country who are enthusiastic about education give us some guidance in this regard at any time. We believe that this is a very meaningful work, and given that publication criticism is not sound today, we should do it with collective power. We are waiting for everyone's enthusiastic response to this request. III. Mail Lending Extended to Other Cities. All readers from other cities who have joined the Reading Guidance Department are entitled to mail lending. However, they must have a regular reading correspondence relationship with this department for one month before they can obtain this right. This has been repeatedly published in earlier issues of this journal. Recently, there are still many readers who have joined this department but have not made a request to borrow books from this department who do not understand that we provide this convenience for readers in other cities. Now, to avoid the trouble of explaining it one by one, we are publicly announcing it again here. If you have joined the research of this department and need us to provide books, you can make a request to this department. We will introduce you to the library's mail lending department according to certain procedures, so that everyone has books to read.

Chunqiu

Fleeting Fragrance of the Imperial Incense 196

— Original Work by Princess Der Ling of the Qing Dynasty, Translated by Qin Shouou

At the same time, Guangxu was extremely optimistic because he knew very clearly that in such an environment, it was as impossible as finding a needle in a haystack to hope to rule. At least as long as the Empress Dowager was alive, he did not have to think about being a comfortable, real emperor again. So he was not sad. He attributed his situation to fate, and in this way, he felt much happier mentally. For example, this time when he went to Fengtian, although he knew that the Empress Dowager wanted to monitor him, he simply thought that he wanted to go out for a tour. Along the way, he freely enjoyed the scenery through the train window. Whenever the train stopped, except for a few of us who had to stay to serve the Empress Dowager, the rest could get off the train and stroll around at will. At this time, Guangxu would often jump down and walk with us. He was very short, with a bit of childishness on his face, but he was not arrogant, and he spoke fluently and pleasantly. He treated us female officials like friends. He probably knew my childhood experiences very well, so he often wanted to talk to me. He asked me about the railways in various European and American countries, as well as the personalities and anecdotes of the monarchs or heads of state of various countries at that time. I only told him the little I knew, and he was very happy and satisfied.

(If I were a real monarch in reality,) he said to me excitedly once, (able to rule the country like the Old Buddha, then the first thing I would do is to follow the methods of the monarchs or heads of state of those foreign countries you told me about and travel around the world. Of course, I also like to travel incognito and don't want people to know my true identity because such a tour is enjoyable. How constrained are we at this moment?) (79)

Queen Bee 197

— Ma Shichi

There has been a beehive on the floor for nearly a year! When I wake up from my afternoon nap, I often hear the bees buzzing, the sound is humorous and gentle, buzzing, making people feel spiritually intoxicated!

In the spring, a bee came, its body was longer than the average, and its color was yellow. This is probably the queen bee! I don't know if the throne was chosen by the bees or taken by force. I won't pay attention to it for the time being, but looking at its shape, it stays motionless in the center of a wax row. Every bee flies around it, as if protecting it, holding small petals in its mouth, and everyone works hard. Their actions are logical, and their lives are strangely fortunate.

One day, a black mountain bee came. It was another species, its body was as big as a cicada, and its shape was terribly ugly. First, it circled outside the hive. It probably saw the comfortable materials and abundant food inside, its eyes gradually turned red, and finally it shrugged its wings and broke straight into the inner layer of the beehive.

Immediately, the orderly crowd stirred up a riot. The queen bee let out a strange cry, miserable and tense, probably giving orders. At the same time, every bee abandoned its small petals and fought fiercely with the mountain bee. The guy, first relying on his strength, also struggled to resist, but he could not withstand the unified and disciplined attack. Before long, he was embarrassed and finally stung and bitten to death alive by the bees. Good! The resistance was successful, order gradually returned, every bee picked up the small petals again, buzzing, always doing that lucky life. At the same time, the queen bee also returned to her central position.

Seeing this battle, I immediately understood that the power of unity is really great, and I also know why the queen bee is supported by her kind. It turns out that she has her own instinct. The throne is not obtained by fluke. At least, she can resist insults and defend the territory!

Mr. Zhu 198

— Chen Jingyu

Mr. Zhu is a rural schoolteacher who sits on the sidelines; because he is deeply trusted by the general villagers, his disciples are indeed quite numerous. However, his own knowledge is very limited; therefore, when teaching and holding a pen, he inevitably has occasional typos and mispronunciations, as well as allusions that are (a donkey's lips don't match a horse's mouth).

The reason why villagers send their children to private schools is nothing more than to want them to recognize a few more names; therefore, the textbooks they use are still those (Three Character Classic), (Thousand Character Classic), (Hundred Family Surnames), (……) and the like. When Mr. Zhu was teaching the compound surname (Mùqí Sima) in the (Hundred Family Surnames), he actually pronounced the two characters (Mùqí) as (Wànshì). Someone said to him: (This should be read as (Mùqí). It is wrong to read it as (Wànshì).) He sternly said: (How can this be?) Don't you see that one ten thousand and two ten thousand in mahjong... isn't that the small (Wàn) character? As for (Qí), it means waiting, everyone knows that. Where is the mistake?) This person saw that he was unreasonable, so he remained silent.

One day, someone asked him to write a contract for learning carpentry, and he actually (didn't decline) and took on the task without hesitation; after he finished writing, everyone who saw it burst into laughter. It turned out that at the end of the contract, he added an incredible classic allusion, (If he can dream up a flowery pen in the future, it will be thanks to the master's gift)! Someone jokingly said: (The ax used by carpenters is not a pen, so it should be said that he dreams up a flowery ax to be appropriate.) At this point, he realized his own misappropriation and immediately blushed; but he still stubbornly argued: (There is still a bamboo pen in the ink fountain used by carpenters; then, it can't be considered completely wrong!)

It is said that he is still sitting and hugging (Gaobi) and living the life of a (Monkey King).

The Northeast Four Company Commanders 199

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 31

Three Times Facing the White-Clad Foes in the Snow Array

The Entire Battalion Sacrificed, Red Eyes Piercing the Gun Forest

Ziqiang shouted from the trench, having fired over a dozen cannons. He muttered to himself, "While there's still breath, I must fight! What's the point of lying in the trench?" He slapped his hands on the edge of the earthen wall and leaped to his feet. The sound of the cannons was indeed more invigorating than any medicine. After this slap, his spirit was completely restored. He jumped down from the bed and ran outside. As he ran out of the house, a cannonball landed right on the roof, collapsing the entire structure. Before the cannonball struck, Ziqiang had already dived to the ground at the first whooshing sound. When the cannonball landed, he was covered in dust. Turning back to look at the house, it was now a pile of rubble. The few soldiers recuperating inside were, needless to say, sacrificed. Ziqiang immediately felt that this body of his was completely salvaged. To stake this salvaged life against the enemy was the most worthwhile thing to do. Thus, he found a fellow soldier, asked where the battalion commander was at the fort, and ran to Baofang, standing tall and giving a military salute. Baofang asked, "Are you completely well?" Ziqiang replied, "I'm well, I can do anything." Baofang said, "Good! You go back to lead your own company. Don't open fire until the enemy is within two thousand meters. Stay calm." Ziqiang agreed and retreated, finding his own brothers. They were like children who had lost their mother's milk, finding their mother again. Although military discipline was in place, everyone expressed their welcome in the smallest of voices, with a booming sound. But they all listened to the acting company commander's orders, each guarding a section of the fort, crouching down and quietly waiting for the enemy. Ziqiang said, "I'm here." Less than five minutes after these words, the black dots of the enemy's shadows were faintly visible in the snowy ground outside the fort. This was unbearable. Machine guns and rifles from the fort began to fire. Since the defending troops were already engaged in defensive warfare, there was no time for concealment. They boldly took a tough stance and returned fire toward the fort. (430)

Small Trinkets 200

— Shiying

Raising a Daughter-in-Law 201

— Gu Pu

Lingxian was a poor family's daughter. At the age of seven, her opium-addicted father sold her to the farming Li family for forty yuan to be their adopted daughter-in-law, meant to be the future wife of Li's second son, Erbao. At that time, Erbao was only three years old, constantly needing to be held and comforted. Lingxian became the nanny for her future little husband. In Lingxian's young mind, there was no concept of "man and woman" or "husband and wife," so she always treated Erbao like her own blood brother.

The wheels of time moved forward incessantly. Lingxian was now eighteen years old. She deeply felt that different changes had occurred to various parts of her body. She heard people talking about matters between men and women, always listening quietly and silently. Sometimes, neighbors would joke with her about her little husband, and she would coyly spit and walk away in shame.

Now, when Lingxian saw her fourteen-year-old little husband, she always felt distant and couldn't avoid him, no longer as intimate as during her nanny days.

Lingxian's in-laws were very happy to see Lingxian growing up like an adult. They planned to marry them off when their son turned sixteen, so they could have a fair and chubby grandson three years later.

But every time Lingxian saw her little husband, she always felt an indescribable sorrow in her heart.

Profiles

Recording Zhang Zhiyu, the Bamboo Carving and Seal Engraving Master 202

— Yangyang

Among the various arts of our country, the origins are earliest, and the successes are numerous. Truly, they are not like the various arts of Europe and America, stealing our leftovers and imitating our old wisdom, and thus are unable to look up to us in the slightest. What is regrettable is that, in our country, most value something only when it is a secret, impossible to transmit. Individuals all like to keep it as their private property, and the habit has been passed down, impossible to correct. If one's son is virtuous, one is lucky enough to preserve and inherit one or two of these skills. If the descendants are unworthy, or their talents and abilities are insufficient, then the person dies, and their art also vanishes. In Europe and America, however, they always do the opposite. Whenever there is a long skill or an invention of any art, they mainly make it public, to seek like-minded people, invent and improve together, and conduct research diligently, making sure the art is glorious, prosperous, and endlessly progressing. In fact, if you examine the source, most of it is plagiarized from ancient Eastern culture, but they are willing to put in hard work and conduct in-depth research. There is Zhang Zhiyu, a famous carving artist from Hebei, who lives in the old capital. He is skilled in calligraphy, capable of writing, and particularly proficient in seal engraving and bamboo carving. He has never been selfish with his art in his life, but always aimed to pass it on, so over the years, countless people have come from his school. The art of bamboo carving began in the Song dynasty, flourished in the Ming dynasty, and the Jiaxing region was the most famous in the Qing dynasty. North of the Yangtze River, it seems there has been no mention of it. Zhang, at the age of twenty, was already immersed and immersed himself in seal engraving and bamboo carving, spending his days silently exploring ancient thoughts, aiming to open up new paths in this art. Since there was no formal mentorship, but imagining things out of nothing, he was able to comprehend the ultimate principles and become a master. Initially, Zhang would visit markets to observe the carving methods on bamboo fan handles sold in the market, which were extremely inelegant. So he would buy them and use his seal engraving knife to repair them, and he was able to master it easily, doing as he wished. Later, he began to carve himself. In three years, he never stopped for a moment. His perseverance and determination were such. His most exquisite carvings were the brick-and-tile rubbings he traced onto bamboo objects. Later, calligraphy and painting became popular on fan bones, and contemporary scholars competed to imitate them. Zhang also began to excel at this, such as the so-called "keeping the green method" and "Xiangfei flower patching," all of which were invented and created by him. "Flower patching" was particularly difficult. Xiangfei bamboo bones are very tender, and when making utensils and fans, the skin is often scratched, which interferes with the original plan for carving calligraphy and painting. However, high-quality bamboo products are a pity to discard, so he had to adapt to the materials and carve flower patterns on the damaged areas. Plum branches are the most suitable carvings for flower patching, so whenever there were damaged items, after Zhang patched and carved plum blossoms, there was not only no drawback of forcing the bamboo to fit, but also a magical touch, truly seamless.

He often said to people in his life: "The way of art is difficult to be elegant but easy to be vulgar. The deeper the skill, the easier it is to become vulgar. It is like rowing a boat upstream, which requires the strength of several people and may not be as expected. Rowing downstream, one person paddling is easy to achieve. This is the difference between vulgarity and elegance." He also commented on bamboo carving: "Elegance is like rowing upstream, which requires more effort, using wisdom and change, and also more knife techniques. It is difficult to describe the elegance of the finished product, only the heart can understand it. For example, if there is an elegant person in front of you, they are no different from ordinary people, and you don't really know where the elegance lies. Only when they face a major crisis without surrendering or a great disaster without being corrupt, then you know their elegance, which can be expressed without reservation. Bamboo carving is also like this, it should have an indelible spirit. Reading it a hundred times without getting tired, there is something to ponder everywhere, this is truly elegant. If you see everything at a glance and then feel disgusted after seeing it again, it is extremely inelegant, and inelegance is vulgarity. A soft brush is difficult to be hard, but hardness is elegant; it is easy to carve deep with a knife, but shallowness is elegant; it is easy to carve shallow with a single knife, but depth is elegant. Like poetry, unusual sentences are better, and something is only valuable after it is difficult to achieve."

Zhang's seal engraving mostly imitates the methods of the ancients, and he made many kinds of copper seal knobs. In the past thirty years, he has carved three or four thousand bamboo pieces and engraved more than ten thousand seals, a truly amazing achievement. The published seal manuals and engravings are titled "Seal Traces," and the carvings mostly imitate the vertical axes and compositions of famous people of ancient and modern times, and they can be so lifelike that viewers do not know that they are engravings. The most exquisite seals are the miniature seals, both spiritual and unique. A work of divine skill, one can only sigh in admiration.

Zhang also created seven kinds of seal paste that do not freeze in winter or leak in summer. The white characters do not reveal the background, and the red characters are not blurred. If you bake it with fire, it turns black as ink but can return to its original color, a truly good product. A certain celebrity in the old capital once wanted to invest money to let him open a store to respond to the needs of the world, but it is not known whether it was actually implemented. However, since Zhang did not keep his achievements secret, his method should have been widely spread in the Tianjin area for a long time.

Mr. Yuan Saiyun, the owner of the Zhe Huan residence, once wrote a couplet to give to him, saying: "Should be combined with the bamboo carvers and seal carvers, directly chasing Zhang Dian and Mi Dian's calligraphy." Dan Weng also gave a poem, saying: "The seal carver is already Yan Chang, the bamboo carver also hopes to be Huang, the calligrapher is the Ershui, the three Zhangs are the same as Zhang." These are all people who deeply admired Zhiyu.

Sports News

Germany Actively Preparing for the Eleventh World Games, Organizing Committee Chairman Details Preparations, Welcoming Athletes and Visitors from All Countries, Stadium Architecture is Grand and Scenery is Beautiful 203

(Special dispatch from Beiping) The Eleventh World Games, scheduled to open in Berlin, Germany on August 1, 1936, China has prepared to participate. The chairman of the organizing committee, Lewald, sent a long letter to Ping today (6th), detailing the mission of the Games and the actual preparations. The main points are excerpted and translated as follows:

The Profound Meaning of the World Games 204

The World Games held in 1932, it is believed, are still remembered by people all over the world. This Games has been held ten times, the first time in Athens. This is the highest ideal, to enable the sports of all countries to follow uniform rules, hoping to have a period of progress every four years. Therefore, it is the most glorious thing in history to enable all nations to have sports relations with each other. Thanks to the support of friends from all walks of life, the World Olympic Games has been consolidated. In addition, there are various literary, musical, and sculptural competitions, and there has been a large-scale construction of sports equipment and cultural medals. There are two great events among them: on the one hand, to improve the competitive spirit of all countries, and on the other hand, to enable the people of all countries to have the idea of strengthening their physique, to have patriotism, knightly bravery, and noble spirit. If so, the benefits to the modern group are not small. All civilized countries in the world should do their best, and governments should also be open and honest, serving the entire world, and should have an attitude of joy, and should no longer have other conflicting international opinions.

Glorious Achievements Over the Years 205

The 1936 World Games - that is, the Eleventh Olympic Games - was decided by the Barcelona International Olympic Committee in 1931 to be held in Berlin, the capital of Germany. Previously, Germany was supposed to hold it in 1916. At that time, it was first held in Stockholm, in order to integrate all Western culture. At that time, everyone had a kind of hope for this 1916 Games, cheering and carrying on, regarding this time (opening in Germany) as serving the emperor of the time. The war broke out at this time, causing it to sink invisibly. The Olympic Games held in Antwerp, Belgium in 1920, and the Olympic Games to be held in Paris in 1924, were also suspended due to the shock of the war. Fortunately, the representatives tried their best to maintain it, and it still exists to this day, without losing its greatness. It was not until 1928 that it was held in Amsterdam, the capital of the Netherlands. This international games brought together countries that were previously enemies, reconciled as before. The spirit of this games is the best thing in the world.

German Government Advocating 206

This time, this event, held in Berlin, can show a deeper and broader meaning. All the people of Germany are looking forward to the arrival of this day, admiring the athletes and spectators from all over the world, who have come from afar to visit. This is the biggest opportunity after the World War. The German nation can take this opportunity to step into the world arena, try out its great creativity, refresh the world's ears and eyes, and know that our ancient civilized Germany has a good cultivation in sports and new ideas of the modern era. President Hindenburg, the honorable general, has allowed to give more protection, and the new government under the leadership of Hitler has also approved and helped as much as possible. Here, the Olympic principles guide all countries with the criteria of striving and creating, so that many unnecessary political struggles in the country can be brought into the right track. There is no racial boundary or religious sect here. Anyone who wishes to participate will be treated equally. The organizers of this conference have made considerable preparations, without any obstacles, and can carry out the whole process in Berlin. The Organizing Committee has established a Supreme Committee, and the Honorary Chairman is the Mayor of Berlin. The German Gymnastics Federation and the Sports League are responsible for preparing the sports equipment. The chairman of the Organizing Committee wrote an article entitled "I want to awaken the youth of the world". This article symbolizes the 1936 Games as a wake-up call. This bell will be issued for the first time when the conference opens on August 1, 1936.

Preferential Treatment for Athletes 207

It does not take long to take a train to Berlin in densely populated Germany. Berlin can accommodate 8 million to 10 million people, so people from other important cities can come here to observe as much as possible. Because Berlin is located in the center of Europe, it has a special good traffic foundation and is the intersection point of the continental traffic routes. Therefore, this worldwide Games will be held here, opening a new era. The Organizing Committee has agreed on preferential treatment measures with German merchant ships and railway agencies, that is, all foreign groups who want to come to Berlin can enjoy low-cost treatment. Berlin has superior hotels, such beautiful hotels, with complete hospitality and everything available, and the price is also quite low. If athletes from a certain country want to rest after the competition, the Organizing Committee has prepared an Olympic Village for them, which is only fourteen kilometers straight from Berlin Central Station. There are dormitories built layer by layer, where they can live freely.

Stadium Architecture 208

Berlin has planned and completed everything else about the Olympic Games. The racecourse and track opened at the bottom of the city in 1916 still exist today. There are lush trees there, created using modern common sense, and can accommodate 100,000 spectators around the perimeter. Other buildings are very grand, but the swimming pool is located elsewhere. Most of the important competition fields are at the Oval. The longitudinal axis of the entire field is 50 meters, and everything in it is explained with diagrams. This Games is of great benefit to Germany. German university students can train their physique on the German sports field and directly connect with all parties. However, in sports buildings or main competition fields, they must not be arbitrary, such as when announcing their withdrawal from the Games, during football games, and during fencing, and when important competitions are held, all prizes are not displayed in the sports field, but placed in a display room outside the field, a ten-minute or twenty-minute car ride from the sports field. As for the artistic competition works of each participant, they are displayed in the hall inside the sports field. This can gather all kinds of Olympic sports products, which is an unprecedented event. Therefore, all athletes, in this crowded conference, do not spend time and energy, and can move their works from their original place to other places. As for the rowing course, it is located at the Grunau Lake, opposite the end of Berlin, which can be reached in three-quarters of an hour. However, it is more ingenious than the Amsterdam waterway in the Netherlands, and can accommodate four or more small boats competing side by side. There are also many German residents here. If a sailing competition is used, there are many boats around the lake in Berlin, which can be used for spectators to appreciate on the lake. There have also been large-scale boat races before, which we can still be interested in. Before the war, Germany held a royal boat race on this lake. The procedure of the Olympic Games is not transmitted orally in the center of the venue, but it is not called out separately, but must enter the venue in order. This straight sailing of the sailboat allows the audience to observe clearly. If we want all the audiences to have a special good impression in Germany this time, we hope that all German sports organizations will actively participate, and it would be better if more than a thousand people participate, in order to introduce the genius of our nation's creation. After the sports competition, a special selection of the strengths of various national groups is attached, performing a parade horse race, or holding a grand concert. This concert is a common thing in Berlin.

Followed by the Opening of the Art Conference 209

We have already decided to continue the art conference competition immediately. The highest point of the world's art creation is attached, and a large-scale carnival performance of theater musicians is held to show the true spirit of the Olympic Games. In this way, the ideals of modern humans can be realized through this conference, and we can also know how our modern German nation is. Moreover, the outstanding ancient Greek history will also float in our minds. Berliners cherish the only pearl, and German scholars can melt the ancient culture of Olympic Greece. We hope that this Olympic art exhibition will be a spectacular sight. Secondly, we hope that foreign visitors, when visiting Berlin, must know that the capital of Germany is the center of German art and spiritual life. Friends who have an interest in music and art, or who have an interest in natural science and industry, can also visit and practice here as much as possible. In terms of historical aspects worthy of commemoration, there are various beautiful buildings. There are palaces in the city and the palace of the people of Charlottenburg. There is a Prussian patron saint in front of the city gate. The museum has magnificent palaces and vast parks. After the Games, trains and private carriages in Berlin will be particularly cheap, and there are also airplanes available for tourists to tour the more beautiful lakes, the scenery in the lakes, and the connected mountains, the Rhine Valley, and to appreciate the birthplace of ancient South German culture.

Education News

The Ministry of Education Again Rectifies the National and Private Universities in Beiping, Cancels the Graduate School of Normal University and Ends the North China College, Peking University and Yanjing University are Commended by the Ministry of Education for Their Efforts in Running Schools 218

(Special dispatch from Beiping) The Ministry of Education's order to rectify the universities in Beiping has arrived in Ping one after another. It expressed satisfaction with Yanjing University and Peking University, and the other colleges and universities have their own criticisms. The rectification of each university is recorded as follows:

Normal University 219

The National Normal University has recently received instructions from the Ministry of Education, with the following four points: (1) The equipment is not sufficiently adequate, the number of staff and security personnel is excessive and should be reduced, and administrative expenses should be streamlined to enhance equipment. (2) There are few full-time teachers, and many important teachers hold concurrent positions and receive concurrent salaries. Concurrent positions should be restricted, and internal part-time teaching should not be compensated. (3) There are too few graduate students and too many staff in the graduate school, with no special equipment, so no achievements can be expected. It should be discontinued starting from the next academic year. (4) To train good teachers for secondary schools, special attention should be paid to moral education. This reporter interviewed the school authorities to ask how they would implement these instructions. It was said that items one, two, and four would be earnestly improved. Regarding item three, the commissioner's report contained inaccuracies. (Note: The graduate school is divided into three departments: the teaching material compilation department, the educational problem research department, and the graduate student training department. The inspector's report stated that there were twelve graduate students and forty-six staff members. It is planned to convene a graduate school committee to discuss the order in detail and request the Ministry of Education to withdraw the decision.)

Peiping University 220

National Peiping University was the first to receive the Ministry of Education's instruction. The main points of the instructions have been detailed in this newspaper's special dispatch from Peiping on the 5th. The merger of the Law and Commerce Colleges will be carried out according to the order. Zuo Zonglun, the dean of the College of Commerce, returned to Peiping yesterday and convened a meeting of department heads and professors at 3 PM today (the 7th) to report on his trip to the south. After the meeting, this reporter interviewed Zuo, who said that he received the Ministry of Education's order about merging the college with the Law College two weeks ago. He went to Beijing the next morning to strongly argue with the Ministry of Education. Minister Wang said there was no way to reverse the decision. He argued further, but it was not approved. He felt it was futile to remain in Beijing and received telegrams from the college's faculty and students urging him to return. He returned to Peiping on the evening of the 6th. The College of Commerce alumni association will hold a meeting today and resolve to (1) send a telegram to the whole country to oppose the merger with the College of Law; (2) issue a declaration detailing the history of the College of Commerce and the reasons for opposing the merger with the College of Law, and seek assistance; (4) contact former presidents and deans of the college, as well as board members before the merger with Peiping University, to jointly protect the college.

Xu Shoushang, the new president of the Women's College of Arts and Sciences, left Beijing on the 6th and is expected to arrive in Peiping tomorrow morning (the 8th) at 8 AM. After arriving, he will hold a college affairs meeting to discuss abolishing the departmental teaching groups.

Peking University 221

A copy of the Ministry of Education inspector's report on Peking University has been sent to Peiping, indicating four points: (1) The number of faculty and staff is excessive. (2) The inspection of student performance and attendance is quite effective, and the responsible spirit of the school's administrative staff is particularly commendable. (3) The College of Science has achieved excellent results. (4) The academic atmosphere is good. Zhu Hong, the secretary of Peking University, stated that the school will comply with the Ministry's order. The method for employing staff will be changed in the next academic year. President Jiang (Menglin) has decided not to renew contracts for staff who are idle in their daily work in order to save money. More than ten staff members have been laid off.

Chaoyang College 222

Based on the inspector's report, the Ministry of Education issued instructions to Peiping Private Chaoyang College, pointing out five points: (1) The low number of absences of teachers and students, and the seriousness of teachers' teaching and students' listening, are quite commendable. (2) The specialized departments should be terminated starting from this year. (3) More full-time military instructors should be hired. (4) The number of students in each class should not exceed the Ministry's quota of fifty. (5) Overly large classrooms are not suitable and should be improved. Wang Jin, the dean of studies at the college, said that the college's specialized departments, up to the 22nd year of the Republic, only included the departments of law, political economics. However, the college has already complied with the Ministry of Education's previous order to close all specialized departments of universities nationwide by the end of the 22nd year of the Republic. There is no need to discuss it again. Although there are many students in each class, they have not exceeded the Ministry's quota, so there is no need to discuss it again. As for hiring specialized teachers and improving classrooms, the college will follow the Ministry's order.

China College 223

The Ministry of Education has instructed Peiping Private China College to make the following reforms: (1) Hire more full-time professors. (2) Change the Department of Physics and Chemistry to the Department of Chemistry. (3) Merge the Department of Commerce and the Department of Economics. (4) Pay attention to the attendance and absence of teachers and students. (5) Improve the equipment of the College of Science. After receiving the order, the college reported to the Ministry of Education that the Department of Physics and Chemistry would be changed to the Department of Chemistry starting this year. As for hiring full-time professors, paying attention to the attendance and absence of teachers and students, and improving the equipment of the College of Science, it can also be done this year. However, merging the Department of Commerce and the Department of Economics is difficult in practice, so it is requested that the Department of Commerce be allowed to continue to exist. It is reported that this document has already been sent out.

North China College 224

North China College has been run well, but it is difficult to develop due to financial difficulties. After the Ministry of Education inspector completed the inspection, the educational aspects of the college were deemed commendable, but the funding was considered too low. Now the Ministry of Education has ordered North China College to close. Zheng Haoran, the dean of studies at the college, went to Beijing to contact President Chu Minyi and the Ministry of Education. It is reported that the college can continue to operate in the next academic year.

Yenching University 225

Yenching University recently received instructions from the Ministry of Education, the original text of which is as follows: The school was inspected by personnel dispatched by this Ministry, and according to the report submitted, after careful review, most of the school's teachers are full-time and can work hard on research. The staff are also conscientious in their work, the financial arrangements are appropriate, and the equipment is adequate. The school provides residences for faculty and staff, providing teachers and students with opportunities to interact. These achievements are commendable. However, the following points still need attention and improvement: (1) The school originally had three colleges, eighteen departments, two specialized courses, and a graduate school divided into twelve academic fields, which is too large. The school is currently experiencing financial difficulties and should strive to consolidate in the following two ways to remedy this situation: (1) The colleges and departments should consider merging and submit a request to the Ministry for approval. (2) The graduate school should reduce its scope and submit a proposal for approval in accordance with the "Provisional Organization Regulations for University Graduate Schools" promulgated by the Ministry. (2) The school's administration and printed regulations are mostly in English, which is inappropriate. In the future, Chinese should be used. (3) The school's student life is often extravagant and should be corrected to cultivate a frugal atmosphere. (4) The school's sources of funding have been declining recently due to the impact of the world economy and are greatly insufficient. Efforts should be made to raise a fixed endowment fund to consolidate the school's economic foundation. It is hereby ordered to comply with the instructions and report back. This order.
