The Municipal Education Bureau's Summer School and Summer Training Class Open 228

More than 400 students attend the opening ceremony

Mayor's representative and Director Pan give instructions

The 4th Summer School and the 2nd Summer Training Class organized by the Municipal Education Bureau of this city held an opening ceremony at 7:30 AM yesterday in the auditorium of Shangwen Elementary School. Present were Secretary Zhang Yuanruo, representative of Mayor Wu, Committee Member Cai Hongtian, representative of the Municipal Party Headquarters, Director Pan, Section Chief Zeng, Supervisor Ma Chonggan, Lecturer Guo Yicen of the Municipal Education Bureau, and more than 400 students from the Summer School and Training Class. The details are as follows:

Ceremony Order 229

(1) Ring the bell to start the meeting. (2) All stand. (3) Sing the Party song. (4) Bow three times to the Party flag, the national flag, and the portrait of the Founding Father. (5) Read the Founding Father's will. (6) Silent tribute. (7) Report on the preparations. (8) Mayor's speech. (9) Representative of the Municipal Party Headquarters' speech. (10) Director's speech. (11) Representative of the lecturers' speech. (12) Photograph. (13) Adjourn.

Preparations 230

After the formalities, Zeng Shengdian reported on the preparations, stating that the Summer School organized by the Municipal Education Bureau is now in its fourth session, and the Summer Training Class is now in its second session. All courses are set according to the regulations of the Ministry of Education and with reference to the situation of schools in this city. The lecturers are all university professors or well-known figures. This year, 328 people have registered for the Summer School and 156 people have registered for the Summer Training Class, totaling about 500 students. The Summer School is located at Shangwen Elementary School, and the Training Class is located at Wuben Girls' Middle School. The Education Bureau has also borrowed Xicheng and Meixi Elementary Schools as dormitories to facilitate those who come from afar to attend. Classes will start tomorrow.

Representative's Speech 231

Secretary Zhang, the representative of Mayor Wu, gave a speech, saying that today, on behalf of the mayor, he hopes that everyone will not think that they are teachers and feel wronged to study at the Summer School. They should know that teaching and learning benefit each other and should make redoubled efforts. Second, do not think that elementary school teachers are suffering and belittle themselves. Third, they must recognize that elementary school teachers are actually undertaking work that reaches the people and break the reasons for the failure of the slogans shouted to the people by social activists in China in the past. Fourth, use ten years of recovery and ten years of education to do the work of truly revitalizing the nation. The first step is the most important elementary school teacher. Everyone should cultivate the seeds of the nation and lay the foundation for the future revitalization of the nation. Next, Cai Hongtian, the representative of the Municipal Party Headquarters, gave a speech, saying that elementary school teachers are the parents who instill knowledge into the future masters of the country. Their position is very high, and they should redouble their efforts to cultivate themselves.

Director's Speech 232

Then, Director Pan gave a speech, saying that everyone has come here during the summer vacation to seek knowledge and make their future work more progressive. The Education Bureau also organizes the Summer School and Training Class for this purpose. Today, I want to talk to you about the meaning of education. The purpose of education is often different under restrictions, but in principle, no matter what region or time, if the education cause does not go wrong, there will always be a common principle or theory, that is, why the elderly should teach the young. The theory is the same everywhere. Now, let me explain with the words of ancient Chinese educators. The Doctrine of the Mean says, "What Heaven imparts to man is called human nature. To follow our nature is called the Way. Cultivating the Way is called education." To run education, we must first know the personality of the child, the nature of the student. This nature is what Heaven imparts to man. All human beings have a common nature, and each person also has a unique personality. The combination of common nature and unique personality forms each person's nature. Nature is the mandate of Heaven, and the mandate of Heaven is nature. Nature is produced by the natural action of metabolism. Talking about education, if you do not understand the student's nature, you are not an educator. The Way is the road. To follow one's nature is to control one's nature and not let it be unrestrained. Being able to follow one's nature is the Way, so following one's nature is called the Way, even if one's reckless nature is controlled and walks in orbit. Cultivating the Way is called education. Educators are laborers who build roads. The road they build is the road of being a person. The road of being a person is built by those who are engaged in education, but the road of being a person only needs to control one's character to have the Way, and educators must always cultivate the Way, especially it is important to start cultivating from a young age. This is the foundation of all education. Finally, after the teacher representative Guo Yicen gave a speech, a photograph was taken and the meeting adjourned.

The Jiangxi Education Department Plans to Establish 400 Zhongshan People's Schools Province-Wide This Year 233

(Nanchang Correspondence) Jiangxi is the province most deeply affected by bandits. The people's thinking is greatly influenced by their negative impact. The authorities have decided to implement special education in the hope of correcting the people's erroneous thinking, training local self-defense, and increasing rural production, so as to achieve the simultaneous implementation of education, cultivation, and health. The Jiangxi Education Department has now first established special education teacher training classes, research classes, and summer training classes. The first batch of graduates has been assigned to various counties in the recovered areas to run Zhongshan People's Schools. The first phase of the school establishment plan stipulates that a total of 80 schools will be established in 20 counties and districts, all of which are required to be fully established within this month. The second phase will continue to train students, and after graduation, they will be sent to work in various counties. It is expected that 400 Zhongshan People's Schools can be established by the end of this year. After the research class students graduate, they will be sent to work in various counties. It is expected that by July next year, 50 counties will have special education instructors. Within three years, all counties in the recovered areas will be able to establish Zhongshan People's Schools and establish special education training officers. This type of Zhongshan People's School is based on the spirit of political and educational integration to improve the rural economy and technology, assist rural self-defense, and promote rural autonomy.

Special Article

Jiangsu Provincial Yangzhou Middle School Tries Out a Junior Girls' Life Skills Class Origin (1) 240

Women's education in our country has a history of several decades, but it has always been an appendage of men's education and has not been valued by people in society. In recent years, laws and regulations stipulate equal educational opportunities for men and women, and women's education has risen from an subordinate position to contend with men's education. What path should it take? This is of great importance to the future of the family and the country. In recent years, due to equal educational opportunities for men and women, schools at all levels have focused on the cultivation of social people and neglected the cultivation of family people. As a result, many women only consume and do not produce, which is not what China needs today. If this continues and no attention is paid, it will harm the family and the country. We believe that the revival of the nation must rely on the development of women's education, and at the same time, we are deeply concerned that today's women's education will become an obstacle to the revival of the nation. Therefore, we advocate that the new trend of women's education in the future should focus on horizontal development and not vertical development. Here are some facts to show the urgency of reforming women's education, and to state the methods and implementation plans for the women's life skills classes that we advocate adding:

(1) At present, women's schools are mired in the principle of equality in men's education, and ignore the differences in physiology and needs between men and women. They focus on the transmission of knowledge and neglect the practice of household affairs. As for female students in co-educational schools, due to uneven levels and differences in abilities, they devote themselves to the study of subjects and rarely have time to pay attention to household affairs. As a result, in fact, women can handle household affairs before entering school, but after entering school, they cannot do anything. Before receiving education, they consume less of the family, but after receiving education, they consume more of the family and become women who are not suitable for the family.

(2) At present, women's schools mostly assign all matters to staff and school workers to handle. Students only enjoy the benefits of life and regard personnel communication as cumbersome etiquette, lazy to practice, and afraid to do it themselves, which invisibly creates bad habits such as dependence, laziness, and simplicity. They have little spirit of hard work and the ability to cope appropriately.

(3) In recent years, women's clothing has been changing every day. As a result, students are also imitating them. They pursue fashion and compete to show off. In their spare time after class, they like to do unnecessary social activities and useless activities. Bad habits follow each other and are now even worse. The school authorities either indulge in the trend or mistakenly believe that the trend cannot be resisted. They ignore it and do not correct it, which leads to the development of romantic, decadent, arrogant, and extravagant bad habits, making the morality of our country gradually decline. In the future, these women will not be able to be virtuous housewives who manage the family, nor will they be able to be kind mothers who care for their children.

(4) The purpose of women learning ordinary sciences is to use them as a foundation for further study of advanced knowledge and as a tool for improving the family's independent livelihood. However, the fact is often the opposite of the purpose. What today's facts tell us is that, except for a few talented women who are ambitious in their careers and can use what they have learned to engage in social services, most women, once they enter the family and have children, often put everything they have learned on the shelf. Social undertakings cannot be participated in due to involvement, and it is not beneficial to improving the family, and it is still useless for seeking a living. What could be more uneconomical than this?

The above-mentioned disadvantages are all facts recognized by society, and are not intentionally pointed out as shortcomings of today's women's education in order to strengthen the credibility of our argument. Nor is it to obliterate the vertical development of all women's education, but to say that women's education should only have horizontal training. The family is the small unit of the society and the country, and the woman is the housewife of the family and the kind mother of the next generation of citizens. Without a good family, how can there be a healthy country and society? Without a virtuous housewife, men will still have worries at home even if they serve outside, and even their careers will be ruined and their character will be degraded. Without beautiful motherhood, no one will model their children's behavior, no one will pay attention to their health, and no one will protect their happiness. The next generation of citizens will receive this bad family education from a young age. What will be the harm to the country and society in the future? Therefore, we believe that the number of women actually engaged in social undertakings is extremely small, and the greatest majority still bear the heavy responsibility of the family. In order to obtain the actual benefits of improving the family and revitalizing the country, the largest majority of women should receive horizontal education and training. Women's education should no longer focus on vertical development, creating a majority of women who only consume and do not produce, putting the family and the country in extreme danger. Furthermore, the good or bad of social customs and habits should be the equal responsibility of men and women. The necessity of improving today's men's education goes without saying. The shortcomings of today's women's education, based on the above, are also undeniable. Since women have lost their nature under bad education, the more developed women's education is, the more romantic and pleasure-seeking women there will be in society. The more such women there are, the worse the social atmosphere will be, and the faster the family will collapse. The cause and effect generate each other, and it will be endless. Therefore, in order to save the declining trends and revive the nation, we do not avoid the general criticism of society and put forward opinions on reforming women's education, and drafted a plan, respectfully inquiring the opinion of enlightened people, and presenting it to the Jiangsu Education Department to first add a junior girls' life school in the provincial Yangzhou Middle School to engage in practical experimentation. The scale is not large, the equipment is not sophisticated, but it is realistic and seeks truth from facts, and establishes a atmosphere. It is hoped that people who are interested in improving women's education will give guidance and support, so that it can be managed perfectly and can be used for observation, so as to be the beginning of saving the bad atmosphere of women's education. If the matter can be implemented and the results are obvious, we are happy, and the future of the family and the country will rely on it. Now the training policy, the main points of the method, and the implementation plan are listed below.

Finance: The Trend of Margin Call Squeeze Becomes More Obvious, Another Surge of 4 Yuan and 2 Jiao 242

The Power of the Bulls is Formidable, Swap Premium is Expected to Rise

The Bears are Anxious, the Market Conditions are Extremely Firm for One Day

News of Wheat Procurement: Standard Price Rises by 89 Points 256

Yesterday, the wheat market showed a consistent upward trend. Due to the prolonged sunny weather and inevitable drought, although wheat production was abundant, rice prices soared, thus boosting the market. Furthermore, reports indicated that the government would procure wheat as a form of relief. In such tense times, this move would only provoke more resentment from the public regarding consumption. However, opportunistic merchants, encouraged by these rumors, naturally became more excited. Therefore, at the opening bell, traders covered their shorts, and outside investors rushed to buy, causing the market to surge. Trading was even more active in the afternoon. Near-term trends leveled off slightly, while long-term trends continued to look promising. Considering the prolonged drought, the market may continue to rise further. As a result, the current month rose by five points, August/September rose by six points, October rose by seven points, and November rose by nine points. Silk and Tea: Summer Cocoons Enter the Market, Increased Imports of Japanese Rayon 261

Reduction in Import Tax on Rayon: Since the amendment and promulgation of our country's new tariff regulations, the import tax on rayon has been reduced. Imports of Japanese rayon have increased. In the past three to four days, Japanese ships have brought over 500 boxes of rayon from brands such as Sakura, Toyo, and Ginger Girl. Japanese merchants are actively selling them secretly. Reportedly, a certain silk weaving factory recently purchased over a hundred boxes. Therefore, European and American rayon sales have seen little improvement.

Spring Cocoons from Jiangsu Province Nearing Completion of Transportation: This year's spring cocoons in Jiangsu Province have all had bumper harvests. The fresh cocoons collected by silk cocoon merchants have all been dried. Recently, over 52,000 dan of spring dried cocoons from Jiangsu Province have been transported to Shanghai. Currently, only over 4,000 dan remain in cities such as Wuxi, stored in warehouses and not yet transported. The rest have all been loaded. European and American Silk Telegrams Show No Sign of Transfer to Shanghai: In the overseas raw silk market, silk factories are currently unable to sell their products, and silk prices continue to fall. New factories in Shanghai have sent telegrams but have not seen any transfers. European sales are quiet, and silk merchants have no interest in purchasing. Yesterday, only Yin Zhuang and others purchased eight bales of yellow and white coarse silk at stable and weak prices.

Summer Cocoons in Zhejiang and Hangzhou are Scarce and of Poor Quality: This year's summer silkworms in various cities and villages in Hangzhou, Zhejiang Province, are all locally bred varieties. The initial season was very good. However, around the time of the great sleep, the weather was unusually hot and dry, and there was no rain in the summer, causing mulberry leaves to wither. The silkworms suffered from hunger and disease, and many were discarded. The new cocoons have already entered the market, but only about 30% are of good quality, and the cocoons are thin and of poor quality. Silk merchants have not yet started weighing and pricing. Farmers and silkworm breeders are preparing to dry and reel their own silk for sale.

New Doupion Silk is of Excellent Quality: This year's spring cocoons in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces are abundant and of excellent quality, and the Doupion cocoons are also good. The new silk reeled by Doupion silk factories is of excellent quality, and demand from India is still strong. The British ship Peel, which departed the other day, carried 18 pieces of new Doupion silk, which were transported to England for transfer to India.

Fine Eyebrow and Pearl Tea Sales Active in France 262

Yesterday, sales of fine eyebrow and pearl tea from Luzhuang and Pingshui to French traders became more active. Top and middle-grade goods from Wuyuan and Tunxi were particularly popular. The entire city traded over 1,800 boxes of green tea. Except for Gongxi, which fell by five to six yuan, the market was generally stable. The black tea market, on the other hand, was slightly sluggish. Trade in goods from Qimen and Fuliang was sparse. Although there were sporadic sales of coarse goods from Hunan and Hubei provinces, prices were expected to continue to fall due to abundant inventory.

Hardware: British Tinplate in Short Supply 263

Since German and French goods entered the Shanghai tinplate market, British goods have been implicitly eliminated. This is because their costs are higher than those of German and French goods. However, American goods, due to their superior quality, remain outstanding. Although prices are more expensive than those of German and French goods, customers are still happy to purchase them. However, in recent days, negotiations for British goods have become increasingly frequent. This is because foreign merchants still remember British goods. As a result, their remaining inventory is decreasing, and the number of buyers is increasing. Therefore, quoted prices have improved compared to before. Ninety-pound boxes are estimated at 15.25 yuan, and 100-pound boxes at 16 yuan. Reportedly, there are only about 100 boxes available, and another 300 boxes are expected to arrive in 20 days as futures.

Free Talk

Worries 265

— Huang Huaibai

In the second act of Bernard Shaw's play *Pygmalion*, when the dustman Doolittle asks Professor Higgins for five pounds for his daughter, Higgins takes out his wallet and doubles the amount to ten pounds. However, the hardworking dustman refuses to accept it, saying the following:

"No, Governor. She's not heart enough to spend ten pounds, and perhaps I haven't neither. Ten pounds is too much; it makes you feel like worriting; then all the happiness is gone. You give me what I asked you for, Governor; not a penny more, not a penny less." (Slightly modified from Lin Yutang's translation)

To ordinary vulgar people, the dustman is either a fool or someone from an almost utopian gentleman's country. In fact, neither is true of the dustman's view; rather, his view comes from his rich life experience. Once the secrets of life are revealed, they all amount to the same thing; money is no exception. The difference between humans and animals is minimal, and some may think that this difference is the addition of (money). However, this explanation is inadequate. Poor people never break this riddle. When there is not much money, they are busy with petty gains; when there is too much money, they worry about how to manage and dispose of it. Starting with worries and ending with worries, decades of life pass by without a moment of peace of mind, which is truly pointless! The instinctive life of other animals is vastly different from our divinely blessed humanity, but they are superior in that they have no worries. Therefore, the last stanza of William Blake's poem about a fly is:

Then am I

If I live, or if I die.

We want to cast aside all worries and be happy flies. However, in this vast world, it is probably impossible to find many people who are completely free of worries in body and mind. Even the tiny fly is proud.

Cooling Off 266

— TK

Shimenwan Woodyard Bridge, July 1934

Gulangyu 267

— Liu Ming

I live in a hotel facing the harbor in Xiamen. When I'm lonely, I open the window and look out. The Western-style buildings and green shade on the slopes of Gulangyu are like someone using painting techniques, clearly displayed on the water across from me, revealing a charming style that captivates the eye. The sound of oars often comes from below the window. Just by sticking my head out, I can see boat after boat of wealthy men and women, dressed in splendid clothes, like flowers adorning the harbor. They are either going from Xiamen to Gulangyu or coming from Gulangyu to Xiamen for fun.

Just by taking a trip to Gulangyu, you will feel that it is indeed suitable for wealthy people to live in. The roads along the coast or climbing up the slopes have a quiet and elegant southern flavor. Some villa windows with white curtains quietly peek at the slowly walking tourists from the sparse branches and leaves of the trees. There is simply no noise from carriages and horses or the hustle and bustle of the city. Perhaps you can only hear the sea breeze slowly passing through the woods all day, and the laughter of schoolchildren floating in the streets in the morning and evening.

When I went to visit, I planned to exchange one or two foreign banknotes brought back from Southeast Asia, because I assumed that banks like HSBC were located in the concession of Gulangyu. However, after searching around, I only found Chinese-owned banks. Foreign financial institutions like HSBC, on the other hand, were located in the comparatively unsafe city of Xiamen. From this, it seems that it is indeed the Chinese themselves who need safety. When I returned from Southeast Asia earlier, I took a ship belonging to overseas Chinese and saw the flag of Great Britain raised when it docked in Xiamen. I felt quite strange in my heart. But after visiting Gulangyu and glimpsing the ancient China, my thoughts of blaming others completely disappeared. I was just thinking:

(Old China, it seems that only your barefooted loving children are still full of longing for you.)

Mr. Yu: Your work (Huang) was sent in May. Because I wanted to publish it when the weather was (hot), I put it in a special place. When it was published on the 6th, it was taken from this special collection. (Torch) When the manuscript was published in early June, the editor was ill and did not pay attention. The letter saying to submit the manuscript elsewhere was probably lost. In addition to stopping the publication of the second half as ordered, I hereby reply publicly to clarify that Mr. did not (submit the same manuscript twice) and to clear up misunderstandings from all parties. - Editor

The Problem of Jin Shengtan's Consciousness 268

— Erye

(Infinitesimal theory) has already hit a wall, and the faces of Jin Shengtan's disciples are a bit collapsed. What opportunity should we find to defend Elder Jin again? Thus, Mr. Yu Yangling's article came out.

Jin Shengtan put *Water Margin* and *Zuo Zhuan* and *Lisao* together, and respected them as (talented books), which has no malice, but is a very correct view, just like today's critics value novels that describe rickshaw pullers. As for (talented books), it's just a common abuse of language by the Ming people, just like today's people say (genius) (great man) at every turn. (See the July 4th Free Talk, Mr. Yu's original text.)

What does this passage mean? Did I say that Jin Shengtan had malice? Did I say that his view was incorrect? I did not! I am only pointing out what kind of consciousness Jin Shengtan belongs to. From the perspective of the noble class, yes, Jin Shengtan is (without malice, but a very correct view). As for (today's critics) or (Ming people's abuse of language) or something, it is naturally correct; but it does not prove that Elder Jin's consciousness does not belong to the noble class. However, Mr. Yu still has an article defending Jin Shengtan's consciousness below.

If Jin Shengtan had used the (consciousness of the noble class) to select books, he would never have selected *Water Margin*. Furthermore, he selected *Water Margin* and deleted the purely story-concatenated one hundred and twenty chapters into seventy chapters. This is a purposeful work, the purpose of which is to expose the darkness of bureaucratic politics, point out the social causes of the Liangshanpo group, and praise the righteousness of the vagrant class.

Indeed, (this is a purposeful work), but unfortunately, the (purpose) mentioned here is only something that Mr. Yu has come up with now in order to defend Elder Jin; Jin Shengtan himself did not say this. Twenty years ago, I read Jin Shenghuan's preface to *Water Margin* (seal Hangu Pass with mud pellets) (that is, use *Water Margin* to stop the chaos of the world). Unfortunately, I have forgotten it now. I still remember a bit of the meaning of other annotations, so I will bring it up for Mr. Yu to see.

Lin Chong was the first to go to Liangshan. His nickname is called (Leopard Head). Why is he called (Leopard Head)? Jin Shengtan's great insight: Leopards eat their parents, which is the same as wicked people without father or king. The bandits on Liangshan are all without father or king, all leopards. Lin Chong was the first to go up the mountain, and also one of the leaders, so he is called (Leopard Head). How different is this saying from what Mr. Yu is saying now! As for the reason why (if Jin Shengtan had used the consciousness of the noble class to select books), (he would never have selected *Water Margin*), Mr. Yu did not say, so I have to omit it). Let's see Mr. Yu's next article:

He wrote Song Jiang in the story as very loyal and righteous, but ridiculed him for wanting to be recruited to the imperial court, making him worthless. I ask, what kind of consciousness is this.

From these few sentences, I almost suspect that Mr. Yu is reading another kind of Jin annotated *Water Margin*. It is true that Jin Shengtan ridiculed Song Jiang, but what he ridiculed is exactly the opposite of what Mr. Yu said, not (very loyal and righteous, but hoping to be recruited to the imperial court); rather, he ridiculed Song Jiang for being very falsely loyal and righteous, deceiving people with the desire to be recruited, and actually willing to be a bandit. I suppose more than just Mr. Yu and I have read Jin annotated *Water Margin*. (I ask, what kind of consciousness is this)? I answer: This is the consciousness of the noble class, without a doubt. Below, after Mr. Yu quoted a large section of Jin Shengtan's words, he said:

This section explains the infinite exploitation under bureaucratic politics and its inevitable results. How can it be said to be out of (the consciousness of the noble class?)

It's really strange. On what basis does Mr. Yu determine that no one in the noble class is against (infinite exploitation under bureaucratic politics)? And on what basis does he determine that opposing (infinite) exploitation also necessarily opposes (limited) exploitation? In fact, among the noble class, there are many who oppose (infinite) and hope for (limited). The earliest were Confucius and Mencius. Confucius wanted people to be good people, and Mencius wanted people to live good lives. There is not a single sentence in their works that supports exploitation; on the contrary, there are many sentences that oppose exploitation. But they all belong to the consciousness of the noble class. Enough small talk, let's copy some of Mr. Yu's quoted Jin Shengtan's words:

Alas! The world is the world of the imperial court, and the people are the children of the imperial court; but now let loose unlimited tigers and wolves, open unlimited greedy mouths, take unlimited muscle, fill unlimited ravines, and want the people not to rebel, and the country not to perish, how can this be!

Full of (imperial court) (imperial court) (I ask, what kind of consciousness is this)? I answer: How can it be said that this is not out of the consciousness of the noble class?

Conclusion:

First, Jin Shengtan's consciousness is the consciousness of the noble class.

Second, it cannot be said that Jin Shengtan's consciousness is not out of the noble class.

Third, Jin Shengtan's consciousness is different from what Mr. Yu has determined.

Liars (3) 269

— Caoming

When the doctor finished the examination and said that the child was already more than two months old, I was so angry that my eyes almost popped out of their sockets. The woman sat there as if numb from exhaustion, recounting without any panic that she had discussed with a sick woman next door—the child's mother—because of hunger. As a result, she spent a few copper coins to buy a bowl of pig's blood and smeared it on the child's head. Then, she carried the child and ran to Pingxi Lane.

(Sir, if you had come one step later, I could have had a full meal tonight, and the child's mother could have had a doctor examine her pulse. (But do you know that you are deceiving people? Do you know that you are breaking the law?)

(Really, I don't know what you mean by breaking the law.)

I remembered the suffering of illiterate people and deliberately explained to her calmly: (The law is to protect the interests of the people and guarantee their peace. For example, now you have broken the law and cheated people out of money. I have to take you to the Public Security Bureau to be punished...)

(Oh, I understand this law. But if I am punished, who is it protecting—why don't you want my interests, sir?)

I scratched my head and said after a while: (Everyone. To prevent everyone from being deceived!) I was very satisfied with my answer.

(Why doesn't the law let me have a good bowl of peaceful food, why doesn't it let the child's mother not be sick? Sir, how dare I say that you are also deceiving me?)

(Quickly carry the child, take the money you cheated, and come with me to the district!) I remember shouting at her like that.

When we turned to the secluded Panfu Road, I stopped, took out the only one yuan note from my pocket, handed it to her, and said to her encouragingly in a low tone: (Consider me unlucky today! But after you go back, you must fix yourself and be a law-abiding citizen!) That's how we parted ways. You can imagine how soft my heart is!

(If I want to play the trick again, where can I bother you for another yuan, sir?) This light sentence was raised behind me. When I turned my head, there was not a single ghost shadow left.

Fusheng, do you plan to do some charity work? Do you think you are saving someone? But you are wrong. You seem not to know the saying: Compassion is squatting at the feet of the law. Understand? Yes, you still need to train more!)

Our district chief said to me like this, and then he honestly started training me. (The End)

Extra Local Edition of Shen Bao

Commentary

Has Science Gone Bankrupt? 270

— Han Bai

Breaking the sixty-year high temperature record, the long days of red light, the blue starry sky, slowly passing day and night. This has shocked the brains and hearts of every farmer in the countryside. It seems that this year will be a year of famine!

As a result, the so-called humanitarians and superstitious people are blowing their (praying for rain) methods. In Jiangyin, led by gentleman Zhu Danqing, they invited the chief of the Public Security Bureau and the county magistrate to participate together. Wuxi, Changzhou... are also similarly prohibiting slaughter and piously hoping that God can show some kindness. What is this phenomenon! We clearly know that this is an era of the 20th century, the era of the most developed science, an era in which people have been liberated from the iron chains of nature's control over humanity. Science tells us that (rain) is a natural phenomenon, formed by water vapor encountering cold. If we want to hope for rain through human power, it will never be effective through superstition and religion. We must use the already developed science to control nature. According to recent Soviet communications: the success of rainmaking machines is a very obvious example.

Then why do the general superstitious fanatics do that? I think they want to greatly reduce the age of the century to hundreds of years ago, so that the people return to the Middle Ages; they want to deny science, no, they want to destroy science. Because science imposes a task of movement on the fate of society; while superstition forever declares the death penalty of the poor masses as slaves.

Undoubtedly, superstition is the spiritual tool of deceivers, and the vanguard of anti-science. In any era, when the poor masses begin to think about the real reasons for their plight, the superstitious people feel very unfavorable. Therefore, in this society, in order to divert the attention of these poor masses from the examination of material life on earth; and to shift the emotions of dissatisfaction with the present world to the hope of the afterlife, superstition is the most powerful tool, which is the fact that history tells us. For example, (praying for rain)! It is very obvious that local leaders are giving the people an empty sesame ball to eat, obscuring the truth that human power can overcome natural control. The face of superstition is most clearly exposed here.

Are we willing to heartlessly let science go bankrupt? Are we willing to be attacked by reactionary forces? No, we should maintain science and defend science, the condition is that everyone bravely raises the banner of anti-superstition.

Praying for Rain 271

— Yafei

The summer in Jiangnan, the sun burns fiercely on the earth; a scorching wind blows through the rural areas and urban alleys of Jiangnan. For the past week, the atmospheric pressure has consistently been above one hundred degrees. Not a single drop of rain has fallen, and people are longing to see the sweet rain. (Hoping for clouds in a great drought!) Rain has become the most precious treasure. In the season of yellow plums, who would have thought there would be such a severe drought? The paths in the countryside have all cracked open. The wind blowing on people is scalding hot. In the desolate wilderness, the leaves on the treetops and the sprouts on the ground have all withered; the seedlings in the fields have all dried up. Farmers have nowhere to draw water from, and can only sigh as they look at the withered seedlings!

Alas! The drought has arrived, and a year of famine is upon us! The harvest for the year is gone; heaven is truly trying to take the lives of the poor!

Isn't that so? Rice prices have suddenly soared in the past few days. In less than a week, they have already increased by three or four yuan per stone. Doesn't this make life even harder for the poor?

One clear morning, the sun had just peeked half its face from the east: Uncle A-liu, with a face full of worry, walked out of a dilapidated thatched hut and went to the open space in front of his door. He saw Jin Gou—his son—and A-cui, the daughter of Old Wang next door, chasing a pair of butterflies in the grass. He glared at them fiercely, ready to vent a bellyful of sorrow on Jin Gou.

"Getting up so early, not staying in the nice house, but coming outside to wander! Not even afraid of the dew, getting your clothes wet, does your mother have time to wash them for you? Anyway, there's no rice today, and the pumpkins are still flowering; looks like you'll have to go hungry! All you know is how to play all day long, and then you cry for food when you're hungry. A-yin is only nine years old, and she helps Mom cut grass for the sheep and gather firewood, unlike you naughty things; soon, you’ll be gone; if this drought continues like this, I'll have to make you a monk."

After he scolded them for a long time, they both made a face at him and slipped into the thatched hut.

He walked along the bank of the pond in front of the village. An endless sandy embankment stretched out before him; a row of drooping willows leaned listlessly on the riverbank. The water in the river had dried up, leaving only a little at the bottom, and the water color had turned red. A foul smell rose directly from the bottom of the river, which was quite unpleasant.

Over there, in the endless fields, the clods of soil had turned white. He shook his head as he looked at this scene. Disappointed grief constantly attacked his heart. He was disappointed; a year's worth of his sweat had been dried up by the sun! He slowly raised his head and looked at the vast sky; there were no clouds, no wind, only an iron-like blue sky, and a round of red-hot sun, gradually rising above the horizon.

Suddenly, he heard news that had just arrived from the tea house in town: This was good news, and anyone who heard it would show a hint of a happy smile on their worried faces.

It was said that the county government had issued a notice today because the weather was severely dry and the people were about to face famine again. All the flowers and trees were about to dry up, so groups of farmers were marching to the county seat to petition for a ban on slaughtering animals and to piously pray for rain. Their only reason was this: praying for rain was not superstitious, because the capital was still asking Master XX to pray for rain. This was because the National Government cared for and loved the people.

The county magistrate and other officials discussed the matter and found no way to refute their reasons. In order to hear the villagers shout "Upright Magistrate," they agreed to ban slaughtering animals for a week. At the same time, they invited Grand Master XX and others to set up an altar in the suburbs about ten miles west of the county seat to pray for rain. They had chosen XX month XX day to open the altar at dawn. Grand Master XX would preside over the altar, leading the entire group of Dharma Masters to piously perform rituals, give speeches, and pray. On this day, the county magistrate, the committee members of the Party branch, and the local gentry would all take time out of their busy schedules to attend. The ceremony would, of course, be extremely grand.

Master XX, wearing his kasaya and holding a sword, ascended the altar, chanting words in his mouth. The other Dharma Masters all echoed him in the same way. The instruments clanged and clattered, shaking the sky. He slammed a spirit tablet in his hand. The scorching sun beat down on their bald heads, and beads of sweat fell like broken strings of pearls. The county magistrate, the Party committee officials, and several famous

Continued on page three

Page 21

Local gentry, however, all sat in sedan chairs and returned to their official residences to fan themselves with electric fans and drink iced soda. All that was left here were seven bald heads and some ignorant villagers. However, one day, two days, three days passed, and the heavens still showed no sign of rain. A round of red-hot sun still glared menacingly at them. In the sky, only some gossamer floated, flying quickly outside the blue sky.

The Dharma Masters felt infinitely ashamed! The county magistrate, the Party committee officials, and the local gentry all showed disappointed faces.

Uncle A-liu, like the other farmers, had a layer of disappointed grief and anxious expressions on his face! It still didn't look like rain would fall any time soon.

Alas! Heaven nourishes people as one raises an elephant, but people need to raise snakes! There's nothing one can do when Heaven wants to take from people. Finally, tearful faces and anxious hearts intertwined and flowed under the scorching sun!

Death of Siblings 272

— Wen Hei

The death of my siblings has brought me grief for the fourth time now!

My third younger sister died when my family was going bankrupt. Since she was a child, she was a lively and playful child. At that time, the family didn't have money to send her to school after she graduated from elementary school, and she was also a student who didn't like sitting on a cold bench listening to poorly taught books by rural teachers. She said it wasn't interesting. She wanted to contract an illness caused by the fatigue of traveling, and treat it so that her chest and heart burned like fire; another so-called famous doctor was changed to use cool medicine to treat it, and she was thus killed alive! From her illness to her death, I was by her side. That kind of tragic situation didn't make me sad, but rather made me resentful. The so-called doctors were actually murderous executioners!

My fifth younger brother died when I left my hometown to study outside. When I heard the news of his death, I cried! Why did he die? He also stayed at home after graduating from elementary school without going to school, and because of this he was stimulated by the family and died of lung disease. He was very gentle. After graduating from elementary school, he went to work as an apprentice in a relative's shop, but he lost his job after half a year and couldn't find anything to do again; when he returned home, his mother—my stepmother—nagged and scolded him all day long, not earning money and only eating, causing him to worry and shed tears and only endure scolding; soon, lung disease developed, and he had no interest in life, so he didn't tell anyone and waited to die. A child in his teens was vomiting blood and waiting to die all day long, but his father didn't know, and his mother didn't care about him, until he died with a bitter smile to his family, what a sad thing this is!

Because of the death of three younger siblings, I often said to my father that he should educate and take care of his younger siblings, but recently I received a letter from home that my tenth younger brother had died again! My tenth younger brother was only seven or eight years old the year I left home—I've been away from home for eight or nine years now—last year he gave me a letter saying that he was about to graduate from elementary school, and I liked him, I often played; but he could make trains, steamships, and guns at home, he was a person with a talent for machine manufacturing. I often said to my father, let my third younger brother go to electrical engineering school, and he will definitely be an engineer in the future; but because of economic reasons, he was not even sent to high school. He liked to play, so he fell ill after falling while playing soccer, but he didn't dare to tell his father that he was injured. A quack doctor in the countryside treated him as an ordinary fever, and when he became seriously ill, he treated him as a cold, until he went crazy and died. Half of his death was his own fault, and half was the quack doctor's fault. At first, I didn't know when I was outside. When I came back to see him when he was critically ill, there was no way to save him, watching him die in the pain of frantic screaming. The death of my third younger sister made me hate quack doctors; but there was also the death of my second younger sister, which made me hate quack doctors even more deeply.

My second younger sister returned to her hometown from a school in a distant place where tuition and board were free during the summer vacation. At that time, I was teaching elementary school in my own village. As soon as she got home, she fell ill. I didn't trust the doctors who were usually invited at home, so I specially invited a so-called famous doctor to see her. Unexpectedly, this so-called famous doctor was also a good-for-nothing. After he took her pulse, he said that she had overworked herself at school and was weak, so he used tonic medicine, giving her a normal

Communicated with him, I told him a lot of knowledge outside of books; this spring, my father reluctantly managed to let him go to the newly established junior high school in his hometown, I sent him two dollars to buy a new pair of shoes to go to school, but unexpectedly he died again because of illness! The father's letter said that because there was no money at home, there was no way to invite a Western doctor, so he was treated by a Chinese doctor, and finally he could not be saved and died! Although the letter did not mention what kind of illness, but, undoubtedly, it was killed by a quack doctor! I loved my tenth younger brother, his kind of seemingly innocent and seemingly silly expression still makes me recall it. When I call out "Second Brother", his eyes are smiling and his mouth is blankly open. I really like him, I really love him, now he is dead, killed by a quack doctor, | my lovely brother yo! I love him, I want to see him again in my dreams!

Once the family goes bankrupt, the economy cannot be maintained, and younger siblings all die at the hands of quack doctors. When will there be that day: public hospitals are set up in every village. The people's diseases are treated by the public, and the people's health is protected by the public? There is only one country in the world now, and the lives of its people are guaranteed. When will we have that day in China?

Due to the death of siblings, dying at the hands of quack doctors, and dying in the absence of money to be healed, I can't help but look forward to the arrival of a perfect society!

Mr. Fan Zhixuan's Works 273

— Fan Zhixuan

Mr. Zhang Mengfei's Works 274

— Zhang Mengfei

Spring and Autumn 275

— Mu Lu

Many people compare fate to the seasons, so who is spring for? Who is autumn for?

There is spring and autumn in the metropolis, there is the fragrant flesh of girls, and there are also the blood and tears of the poor...

It is said that people who are used to living in the city don't know much about the changing seasons. I don't know what that means? But I just think to myself: the young ladies' powder legs are less trembling on the street, maybe spring is gone, but I see the yellow water flowing straight down between the unshaven hairs of the rickshaw pullers, I gaze at the blue clouds in the sky for a while, and I wonder if it's spring or autumn now!

Continued on page five

Page 22

Page 23

Although, there are tender green tung trees, beautiful flowers and plants, singing birds, and moonlight that doesn't cost money to buy in my hometown, but these days, the farmers are planting so hard that they are about to plant their lives! There's no way, I have to drag my wife and two children to the city!

When I came to the city, I saw the surging crowd like a tide, and there were very few people wearing blue coarse cloth. My wife bit my ear and said: (The women here have really old faces…) I also savored this trick, the women hanging on the men and running all over the street.

At night, the ghost fire flashes its eyes, and there are countless fire dragons, the two children jump up happily, and I also show a shallow smile on my bitter face, maybe I will walk into spring from now on?

The first time I did business, I followed Brother A-ba to pull a yellow-haired foreigner behind the car. When he didn't want to pay and wanted to leave, I wanted to reason with him, but I didn't know that he would slap me sideways, and then kick me. I looked at the Chinese people who were grinning at us, I looked at Brother A-ba who was holding back his tears, my heart was about to explode!

Now I stroked my hard beard, pinched my dry arms and legs, and thought of my dead wife and the two children who had been sold! I took the wrong path of this city's evil! Where is my spring?

Where is my spring? But I don't believe that God's spring is only for the rich!

Amateur Mailbox

Lifelong Companion 276

Dear Editor:

I am incompetent and have shallow knowledge. Regarding the issue of a lifelong companion, I earnestly ask you to guide me in your spare time. I am now a student in school. My father insists on arranging a marriage for me with a woman who belongs to the old etiquette, but I already have someone in mind. She has received a higher elementary school education, and her love seems to be very dedicated on the surface, but she is too free and often restless at home, likes to do bamboo city plays, and has recently learned to dance. Because of this, I am very mentally distressed. I have given her loyal advice, but she does not change slightly because she loves me. As for the woman of the old etiquette, she is my neighbor, a person I have known since childhood is very honest, but unfortunately she is illiterate and has no common sense. However, she can fulfill her duties as a woman and has quite a bit of the three obediences and four virtues. However, a lifelong companion in life is a matter of a lifetime, and whether the marriage is happy or not is related to lifelong happiness. It is difficult to govern those with knowledge, and easy to govern those who are illiterate; but this matter is important, and I dare not determine which one can have a satisfactory ending. Therefore, I ask

Sir for guidance in a short period of time, I am very grateful.

Respectfully,

Cheng Rong

Answer: If marriage is only seen as the satisfaction of sexual desire, and the union of men and women, then there is no problem, and it is possible to marry anyone. (But humans are not beasts and the harmony of flesh is not enough to satisfy their higher demands than desire. Here, there must be spiritual harmony and attraction between those who want to unite with him.) (Shabel, Women and Society) We should carefully consider whether the bodies and minds of both parties can be harmonized for those who unite. So the (lifelong companion) question you raised is indeed worthy of discussion, but I cannot agree with you taking (1) modern women and old-fashioned women, (2) education level, (3) which is easier to govern as the basis for selection. Your desire to govern women is completely speaking from the position of male dominance. This concept of women as tools should not exist at all now. Being influenced by new ideas and education level is only a condition that the interests of both men and women can be close to each other. Whether it can make each other's spirits harmonize still depends on the entire, subjective purpose and thought of both parties, and cannot be mechanically determined. Although you quite like that (lover), you also hate her liking (bamboo city plays) and (dancing). These are all things that make your spirits unable to harmonize. You only dislike that woman of the old etiquette for not having common sense and being illiterate, but you didn't say whether there is a conflict in your interests and thoughts. From my observation, you seem to be quite able to harmonize with her spiritually, because you are not a non-old etiquette man! The reason is not because you oppose your lover dancing and playing mahjong, no one can agree with her kind of low-level love for enjoyment. You judge who is a lifelong companion with the psychology of governing women, which is completely naked and you are full of old etiquette. I think you should still marry the woman of the old etiquette. Perhaps you can be close in thought and life, but this is because you are easy to govern her. It is absolutely impossible to tolerate male dominance over women.

Editor.

Novel

Lan Jiabao's Mood (3) 277

— Xi Jun

Counting, counting, almost four or five songs have passed. The tall man in the black robe always has such a lonely face; one hand supports his chin, the other hand holds a cigarette, his eyes are quietly staring at the floor, without moving. Smoking, showing the smoke rings exhaled from his mouth, the dark coffee squats on the table, after smoking, he drinks coffee, after drinking coffee, he smokes again, always sitting there silently, his lips are like sealed, he doesn't say a word, he doesn't laugh either. It's been the time of four or five songs! Every song has someone dancing with her, and Tian Ren stood in front of her for a while with a smiling face. But how she responded, she always looked at you with two calm eyes, without any expression, and then threw down the cigarette in her hand, slowly propped herself up, shook the hem of her clothes halfway down, and then, as if unwilling, let you hug her and danced away.

(How can a lively person have such a melancholy look?) I asked myself in my heart.

Watching her not talking to the man, Carl also aroused curious attention, because such a person is really not easy to see!

(Wherever she dances, four pairs of eyes chase her.)

Carl watched and sighed:

| This kind of sorrow must not be sorrow for life, look at her never missing a piece of music. | She's another tired person in life!

| That's right, under the grindstone of life, it will often make such a lively person become melancholy.

| Like us together.

| The young man's frustrated mood!

| The young man's frustrated mood!

They both sighed deeply.

I will also be melancholic for her melancholy for no reason! Dazed, under the dark red lights, through a layer of heavy fog, I glanced at the tall man in the black robe dancing across there; still those calm eyes, and also pretty eyes, even more dazzling, and closed clam-like little red lips...

(The young man's terrible frustrated mood!)

I read heavily in my heart again.
